	<Folder>
		<name>Wine Regions of the World</name>
		<description>This collection of bookmarks depict all wine regions in the world. A wine region is a geographical unit where vine plants (Vitis vinifera) are planted in order to produce wine. Usually, a wine region comprises an area with a homogeneous or similar soil / climate binome. Add to it the cultural practices of the vinegrowers and the winemaking habits of winemakers and you have what the french call «terroir». Usually, a wine region is defined by law. Still, in many countries, it is mostly defined by tradition which will eventually one day result in a legal text.

The scope of this work is to let you pinpoint on the globe the place that produced the grapes which were made into the wine you may be sipping right now and...hopefully, attract you to pay a visit to it. Remember wine is not only food. It is, above all, a cultural object that bespeaks of the region and the men and women behind its making.

Antonio Rocha Graça, 2006</description>
